207	def add_namespaces(metadata: Mapping[str, Any], namespaces: MutableMapping[str, str]) -> None:
208	    """Collect the provided namespaces, checking for conflicts."""
209	    for key, value in metadata.items():
210	        if key not in namespaces:

212	        elif namespaces[key] != value:
213	            raise ValidationException(

215	                " and {value!r}."
216	            )
217	
218	
219	def collect_namespaces(metadata: Mapping[str, Any]) -> dict[str, str]:
220	    """Walk through the metadata object, collecting namespace declarations."""
221	    namespaces: dict[str, str] = {}
222	    if "$import_metadata" in metadata:
223	        for value in metadata["$import_metadata"].values():
224	            add_namespaces(collect_namespaces(value), namespaces)
225	    if "$namespaces" in metadata:
226	        add_namespaces(metadata["$namespaces"], namespaces)
227	    return namespaces
228

253	
254	    if not isinstance(schema_doc, MutableSequence):
255	        raise ValidationException("Schema reference must resolve to a list.")

237	    """
238	    Load a schema that can be used to validate documents using load_and_validate.
239	
240	    :returns: document_loader, avsc_names, schema_metadata, metaschema_loader
241	    """
242	    metaschema_names, _metaschema_doc, metaschema_loader = get_metaschema()

246	        for k, v in metaschema_loader.cache.items():
247	            if k not in cache:
248	                cache[k] = v
249	        metaschema_loader = Loader(
250	            ctx=metaschema_loader.ctx, cache=cache, session=metaschema_loader.session

261

263	    document_loader = Loader(schema_ctx, cache=cache)

265	    # Make the Avro validation that will be used to validate the target
266	    # document
267	    avsc_names = make_avro_schema(schema_doc, document_loader, metaschema_loader.vocab)
